C\u00f4ng ty n\u00e0y k\u00fd k\u1ebft h\u1ee3p \u0111\u1ed3ng \u0111\u1ed1i t\u00e1c v\u1edbi Walgreens, m\u1ed9t chu\u1ed7i c\u1eeda h\u00e0ng d\u01b0\u1ee3c ph\u1ea9m l\u1edbn, v\u00e0 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u00e1nh gi\u00e1 h\u00e0ng t\u1ef7 \u0111\u00f4 la.\n\n\u2022 Khi S\u1ef1 Th\u1eadt B\u1eaft \u0110\u1ea7u \u0110\u01b0\u1ee3c H\u00e9 L\u1ed9\n\nTuy nhi\u00ean, s\u1ef1 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng v\u00e0 uy t\u00edn c\u1ee7a Theranos b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u b\u1ecb nghi ng\u1edd khi c\u00e1c b\u00e1o c\u00e1o b\u00ean ngo\u00e0i b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u \u0111\u1eb7t c\u00e2u h\u1ecfi v\u1ec1 t\u00ednh ch\u00ednh x\u00e1c c\u1ee7a c\u00f4ng ngh\u1ec7 x\u00e9t nghi\u1ec7m c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd. S\u1ef1 th\u1eadt cu\u1ed1i c\u00f9ng b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u ph\u01a1i b\u00e0y khi The Wall Street Journal c\u00f4ng b\u1ed1 lo\u1ea1t b\u00e0i b\u00e1o v\u1ec1 c\u00e1c v\u1ea5n \u0111\u1ec1 trong c\u00f4ng ty v\u00e0 c\u00f4ng ngh\u1ec7 c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd.\n\n\u2022 S\u1ef1 S\u1ee5p \u0110\u1ed5 v\u00e0 H\u1eadu Qu\u1ea3\n\nV\u1ee5 l\u1eeba \u0111\u1ea3o Theranos l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t trong nh\u1eefng v\u1ee5 l\u1eeba \u0111\u1ea3o l\u1edbn nh\u1ea5t trong ng\u00e0nh y t\u1ebf. Switzerland is famed for its breathtaking Alpine scenery, azure lakes, quaint medieval towns and thriving economy. Below are the top 4 destinations in Switzerland:\n\nThe city of Lucerne \nThe city of Lucerne is situated on the shores of the picturesque Lake Lucerne, home to the world-famous Chapel Bridge. The old town\u2019s architecture dating back to the 17th century, clock tower, lion statue, makes Lucerne an idyllic tourist city. It is a paradise for skiing and mountaineering. Visitors can admire Zermatt\u2019s breathtaking views from atop Gornergrat at 3,089m when taking the cable car ride. The traditional wood houses with red rooftops make a memorable impression.\n\nInterlaken\nInterlaken is a popular resort town nestled between two jewel-toned lakes, Thun and Brienz.
